focus_tree = {
	id = YUN_focus_tree

	country = {
		factor = 0

		modifier = {
			add = 100
			tag = YUN
		}
	}

	default = no

	continuous_focus_position = { x = 4300 y = 2500 }

	shared_focus = UPC_the_road_to_unification

	#Coalition Focuses
	shared_focus = UPC_affairs_of_the_ruling_coalition

	shared_focus = UPC_calls_for_a_constitutional_convention

	#Foreign Policy Tree
	shared_focus = KMT_lead_the_liberation_of_asia
	shared_focus = CHN_return_to_the_world_stage_focus

###- Phase 1 -###

	focus = {
		id = YUN_maintaining_the_paradigm
		icon = GFX_focus_DEN_limited_regulations
		cost = 5

		x = 60
		y = 0

		available = { hidden_trigger = { always = no } }
		allow_branch = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = CHN_setup_economic_devastation_early_flag
				has_country_flag = CHN_setup_economic_devastation_normal_flag
				#Phase IV econ starts with these flags
			}
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			base = 100

			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				GXC_ai_factor_prioritize_economic_focuses_trigger = yes
			}
		}

		completion_reward = {
			log = "[GetLogRoot]: Focus Completed YUN_maintaining_the_paradigm"
			custom_effect_tooltip = YUN_black_monday_tt
		}
		search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_POLITICAL }
	}

	focus = {
		id = YUN_alleviate_the_gentry
		icon = GFX_goal_bag_of_money
		cost = 5

		relative_position_id = YUN_maintaining_the_paradigm
		x = -1
		y = 1

		prerequisite = { focus = YUN_maintaining_the_paradigm }

		mutually_exclusive = {
			focus = YUN_centralising_taxation
		}

		available = {
			NOT = { has_completed_focus = YUN_kunming_to_guiyang }
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			base = 100

			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				GXC_ai_factor_prioritize_economic_focuses_trigger = yes
			}
		}

		completion_reward = {
			log = "[GetLogRoot]: Focus Completed YUN_alleviate_the_gentry"
			add_stability = 0.05
			add_war_support = 0.05
			YUN_HRY_medium_effect = yes
			#This branch basically gives you good long term dev.
		}
		search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_POLITICAL FOCUS_FILTER_STABILITY FOCUS_FILTER_WAR_SUPPORT }
	}

	focus = {
		id = YUN_expanding_tin_exports

			}

	}

			}
		}
		search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_INDUSTRY }
	}

	focus = {

			custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = YUN_abysmal_economy_idea2
				add_idea = YUN_abysmal_economy_idea3
			}
			add_timed_idea = {
				idea = YUN_local_industrialisation_efforts
				days = 180
			}
		}
		search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_INDUSTRY }
	}

			}

				}

###- Phase 3 -###

	focus = {
		id = YUN_begin_grand_southern_reconstruction_project
		icon = GFX_goal_SZC_dujiangyan_irrigation_system
		cost = 5

		relative_position_id = YUN_kunming_to_guiyang
		x = 0
		y = 4

		available = { hidden_trigger = { always = no } }

		prerequisite = {
			focus = YUN_develop_yunnans_smelting_company
			focus = YUN_promoting_self_sufficiency
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			base = 100

			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				GXC_ai_factor_prioritize_economic_focuses_trigger = yes
			}
		}

		completion_reward = {
			log = "[GetLogRoot]: Focus Completed YUN_begin_grand_southern_reconstruction_project"
			custom_effect_tooltip = YUN_econ_unlock_tt

					limit = { NOT = { has_tech = CAS1 } }

						limit = { NOT = { has_tech = early_fighter } }

						uses = 1

					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_tech = basic_small_airframe } }
					if = {
						limit = { NOT = { has_tech = iw_small_airframe } }
						set_technology = { iw_small_airframe = 1 }
					}
					set_technology = { basic_small_airframe = 1 }
				}
				else = {

						name = YUN_reorganising_the_airforce
						bonus = 1
						uses = 1
						category = light_air
					}
				}

			}
		}
		search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_AIRFORCE_BONUS }
